style="width: 40px;"></span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif; font-size: 36px;">Aquaconscious</span></strong></h1>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Presented by Chloe Toda, Kaelyn Henzey, Luka He, and Vaidehi Murthy&nbsp;</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;Large-scale AI Data Centers can take millions of gallons daily as a coolant for preventing hardware failures, and more is indirectly used for generating electricity. Queries presented by users to AI chats take only a fraction of this, but e</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">very query, no matter how small, contributes to the overall water consumption.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">The problem isn&rsquo;t a single person&rsquo;s usage, but the culmination of millions of users&rsquo; queries.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;Did you know that roughly&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:700;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">14.33 million liters of water</span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp;are used by Gemini Flash 2.5 alone each day? This is spread across the platform&apos;s 40 million daily users. This is enough water to fill about 130 swimming pools.&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2 dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:8pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:13.999999999999998pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:700;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">The problem: overuse</span></h2>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;People ask AI for everything, from basic math and facts to writing emails. Each unnecessary AI query wastes water that could be used elsewhere, such as for drinking water or growing plants.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">When not to use AI:</span></p>

<div dir="ltr" style="margin-left:0pt;" align="left">

<table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%;">

<tbody>

<tr style="height:139pt;">

<td style="border-left:solid #dddddd 0.75pt;border-right:solid #dddddd 0.75pt;border-bottom:solid #dddddd 0.75pt;border-top:solid #dddddd 0.75pt;vertical-align:top;padding:5pt 5pt 5pt 5pt;overflow:hidden;overflow-wrap:break-word;">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Use Google for:</span></p>

<ul style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;padding-inline-start:48px;">

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Basic facts</span></p>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Weather forecasts</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Store hours</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Contact information</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Definitions</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Searching for recipes or locations</span></p>

</li>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Use a Calculator For:</span></p>

<ul style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;padding-inline-start:48px;">

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Math problems</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Budget calculations</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Calculating tips</span></p>

</div>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">When is AI appropriate?</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Use discretion, but generally, it may be okay:</span></p>

<ul style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;padding-inline-start:48px;">

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">as a research assistant or data analyst, but always check credibility&nbsp;</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">generating ideas or sources for a topic, but not assisting in content creation&nbsp;</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">when assisting, if a personal limitation prevents completing a task</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">for summarizing large amounts of data or reading</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">for getting support with an unknown topic, such as a new language or complex idea, when no other help is available</span></p>

</li>

</ul>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Before asking AI, be sure to ask, &ldquo;Do I actually need AI for this, or could I get this information somewhere else?&rdquo;</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">When you feel you need to use AI, be sure to:</span></p>

<ul style="margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;padding-inline-start:48px;">

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Combine your thoughts: instead of multiple short questions, combine them into a more detailed prompt</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Be specific: a precise query is more efficient and allows for less processing</span></p>

</li>

<li dir="ltr" style="list-style-type:disc;font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;" aria-level="1">

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Save past queries: save useful responses to avoid asking the same questions&nbsp;</span></p>

</li>

</ul>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:normal;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Your digital choices have real-world consequences. Every unnecessary AI question wastes water someone else needs.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p dir="ltr" style="line-height:1.38;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:8pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:Verdana,sans-serif;color:#000000;background-color:transparent;font-weight:400;font-style:italic;font-variant:normal;text-decoration:none;vertical-align:baseline;white-space:pre;white-space:pre-wrap;">Make it count!</span></p>
